  export class $my_collector<Item extends { id: ()=>string }> extends $mol_object2 {

    constructor(
      public state: ()=> $mol_state_shared,
      public item: (id: string) => Item,
    ) { super() }

    items(next?: Item[]) {
      const ids = this.ids(next && next?.map( obj => obj.id() ))
      return ids.map( id => this.item(id) )
    }

    ids(next?: string[]) {
      const ids = this.state().list(next)
      return ids.map(String)
    }

    add() {}

    drop() {}

    find() {}

    filter() {}

    has() {}
  }

}
